SELECT id AS up_id,  ra AS up_ra,  dec AS up_dec FROM MYDB.input_sample  CREATE TABLE #tmp (   up_id varchar(#),   objid bigint ) INSERT INTO #tmp EXEC spGetNeighbors #    INSERT INTO MYDB.output_sample SELECT a.id, a.ra, a.dec, t.objid as matched_id, s.specObjID, s.plate, s.mjd, s.fiberID, s.ra, s.dec, s.z, e.EW_Hb_#, e.EW_Hb_#_Err, e.Flux_Hb_#,   e.Flux_Hb_#_Err, e.EW_OIII_#, e.EW_OIII_#_Err, e.Flux_OIII_#, e.Flux_OIII_#_Err, e.EW_Ha_#, e.EW_Ha_#_Err,  e.Flux_Ha_#,   e.Flux_Ha_#_Err, e.EW_NII_#, e.EW_NII_#_Err, e.Flux_NII_#, e.Flux_NII_#_Err, e.sigmaStars, e.sigmaStarsErr, e.Sigma_OIII_#, e.Sigma_OIII_#_Err,    e.Sigma_Ha_#, e.Sigma_Ha_#_Err		 FROM #tmp t   JOIN MYDB.input_sample a ON t.up_id = a.id   JOIN specobj s ON s.bestobjid=t.objid   JOIN emissionLinesPort e on e.specObjID = s.specObjID WHERE s.class = &&&
